			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> &nbsp; &nbsp;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#x201C;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">We know we will probably face some </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">challenges in the coming weeks and months as we continue to operate a global business through these volatile and uncertain times.&nbsp;&nbsp;But we are a strong tribe and an enduring company.&nbsp;&nbsp;W</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">e &nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">are confident that we are well positioned to navigate this storm as it unfolds from </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">both </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">a financial and operational perspective and emerge on the other side a stronger company,&#x201D; concluded Ridge.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0.1pt 0pt;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">&#xFEFF;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">

		</p>

		<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;;font-size: 10pt"><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;"></font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0.1pt 0pt;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">Other Significant Financial Developments</font>
		</p>
		<div style="width:100%"><table style="width:100%; table-layout: fixed;" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0"><tr><td style="width:18pt;"><p style="width:18pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td valign="top" align="left" style="width: 18.00pt;">
			<p style="line-height:115%;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:0pt;">
				<font style="margin:0pt;font-family:Symbol;line-height:115%;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9;font-size:10pt;;"> &#xB7;</font>
			</p>
		</td><td style="width:0pt;"><p style="width:0pt;width:0pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td align="left" valign="top">
			<p style="line-height:115%;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:0pt;">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">The Company entered&nbsp;into&nbsp;an&nbsp;Amended&nbsp;and&nbsp;Restated&nbsp;Credit&nbsp;Agreement </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">with Bank of America </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">in March 2020 to extend the maturity date of its revolving credit facility to 2025</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> and</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> increase the revolving commitment to $150.0 million. S</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">ubsequently, </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">the Company drew an additional $80.0 million </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">in U.S. Dollars </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">under this line of credit agreement, bringing the balance on the line of credit to approximately $149.0 million.&nbsp; </font></p></td></tr></table></div>
		<div style="width:100%"><table style="width:100%; table-layout: fixed;" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0"><tr><td style="width:18pt;"><p style="width:18pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td valign="top" align="left" style="width: 18.00pt;">
			<p style="line-height:115%;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;color:#000000;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:0.1pt 0pt;">
				<font style="margin:0.1pt 0pt;font-family:Symbol;line-height:115%;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;;"> &#xB7;</font>
			</p>
		</td><td style="width:0pt;"><p style="width:0pt;width:0pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td align="left" valign="top">
			<p style="line-height:115%;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;color:#000000;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:0.1pt 0pt;">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">Management has elected to suspend the stock purchases </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">being executed</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> under </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">the Company&#x2019;s</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">current share buy-back plan.</font></p></td></tr></table></div>
		<div style="width:100%"><table style="width:100%; table-layout: fixed;" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0"><tr><td style="width:18pt;"><p style="width:18pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td valign="top" align="left" style="width: 18.00pt;">
			<p style="line-height:115%;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;color:#000000;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:0.1pt 0pt;">
				<font style="margin:0.1pt 0pt;font-family:Symbol;line-height:115%;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;;"> &#xB7;</font>
			</p>
		</td><td style="width:0pt;"><p style="width:0pt;width:0pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td align="left" valign="top">
			<p style="line-height:115%;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;color:#000000;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:0.1pt 0pt;">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">Management </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">has withdrawn</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> previously issued full fiscal year 2020 earnings guidance due to the rapidly evolving situation and impact of </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">the COVID-19 health crisis</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">.</font></p></td></tr></table></div>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#xFEFF;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#x201C;Today we are withdrawing our fiscal year 2020 guidance because the </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">current health crisis</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> has injected a measure of uncertainly into our business</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">,</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> which makes </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">it very difficult for us to accurately </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">forecast short-term financial results </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">for the company</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">,</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#x201D;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> said Jay Rembolt, WD-40 Company&#x2019;s vice president and chief financial officer. &#x201C;We are dealing with an unprecedented and </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">extremely </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">fluid situation</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">.</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#x201D;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> &nbsp; &nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#xFEFF;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#x201C;However, the good news is that </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">the company&#x2019;s financial position and liquidity remain strong. We believe our efficient business model and the recent steps we have taken to strengthen our balance sheet leave us positioned to manage our business through this crisis as it continues to unfold,&#x201D; continued Rembolt. </font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#xFEFF;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#x201C;In March,</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> we amended our revolving credit agreement and elected to draw down an additional $80.0 million under the agreement.&nbsp; </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">Though we are already fairly well capitalized, we decided to exercise an abundance of caution and draw on </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">substantially all of </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">the remaining balance </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">on our line </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">of credit to ensure liquidity and manage potential risks during</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> this period of unprecedented macroeconomic uncertainty.&#x201D; </font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color:yellow;">&#xFEFF;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#x201C;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">In addition, </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">we have</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> elected to</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> suspend the stock purchases we are making under our current share buy-back plan in order to preserve our cash</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> until we have a better idea of the long-term financial impacts of this crisis</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">,&#x201D; concluded Rembolt.</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> &nbsp; </font>
		</p>

			<p style="line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;color:#000000;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:0.1pt 0pt;">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">Net sales of maintenance products, which are considered the primary growth focus for the Company, </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">de</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">creased 1 percent in the second quarter when compared to the prior year fiscal </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">quarter</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">.&nbsp; </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">This was primarily attributable to </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">de</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">creased sales of </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">WD-40 Multi-Use Product within Asia-Pacific</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">.&nbsp;&nbsp;Sales of WD-40 Multi-Use Product declined 74</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> percent</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> in China</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">during the second fiscal quarter </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">due to disruptions related to the government&#x2019;s response to the public health crisis caused by </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">COVID-19</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">.</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;color:#000000;"> &nbsp; &nbsp;</font></p></td></tr></table></div>
		<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#xFEFF;</font>
		</p>
		<div style="width:100%"><table style="width:100%; table-layout: fixed;" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0"><tr><td style="width:18pt;"><p style="width:18pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td valign="top" align="left" style="width: 18.00pt;">
			<p style="line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;color:#000000;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:0.1pt 0pt;">

			<p style="line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;color:#000000;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:0.1pt 0pt;">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">Net sales of homecare and cleaning products </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">de</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">creased </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">1</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> percent in the second quarter when compared to the prior year fiscal </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">quarter</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">. &nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">The </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">homecare and cleaning products, particularly those in the United States, are considered harvest brands providing healthy profit returns to the Company and are becoming a smaller part of the business as net sales of multi-purpose maintenance products grow per the execution of the Company&#x2019;s strategic initiatives.&nbsp; </font></p></td></tr></table></div>

			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">Dividend and Share Repurchase </font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">As previously announced, WD-40 Company&#x2019;s board of directors declared on Tuesday, </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">March 17</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">, 20</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">20</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> a quarterly dividend of $0.6</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">7 &nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">per share payable </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">April 30</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">, 20</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">20</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> to stockholders of record at the close of business on </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">April 17</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">, 20</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">20</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#xFEFF;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">On June 19, 2018, the Company&#x2019;s Board of Directors approved a share buy-back plan. Under the plan, which became effective on September 1, 2018, the Company is authorized to acquire up to $75.0 million of its outstanding shares through August 31, 2020. The timing and amount of repurchases are based on terms and conditions as may be acceptable to the Company&#x2019;s Chief Executive Officer and Chief Financial Officer and in compliance with all laws and regulations applicable thereto. During the period from September 1, 2018 through February 29, 2020, the Company repurchased&nbsp;227,529 shares at a total cost of&nbsp;$39.3&nbsp;million under this $75.0 million plan.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">&#xFEFF;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">Withdrawal of Fiscal Year 2020 Guidance </font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Symbol;color:#000000;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">Due to the rapidly evolving</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;"> &nbsp;s</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">ituation associated with</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;"> the </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">global health crisis caused by COVID-19</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;"> and its impact on the global economy</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">, management has </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">elected</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;"> to withdrawal the fiscal year 2020 guidance which </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">was</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;"> reiterated on January 9, 2020.&nbsp;&nbsp;The extent to which the </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">global health crisis</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">will </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">impact the Company&#x2019;s financial results and operations for fiscal year 2020 will depend on future developments, which are highly uncertain and cannot be predicted, including new information which may emerge concerning the severity of the outbreak and the international actions being taken to contain and treat it.</font>

		<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">About WD-40 Company</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0.1pt 0pt;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">WD-40 Company is a global marketing organization dedicated to creating positive lasting memories by developing and selling products that solve problems in workshops, factories and homes around the world. The Company markets its maintenance products and homecare and cleaning products under the following well-known brands: WD-40&#xAE;, 3-IN-ONE&#xAE;, GT85&#xAE;, X-14&#xAE;, 2000 Flushes&#xAE;, Carpet Fresh&#xAE;, no vac&#xAE;, Spot Shot&#xAE;, 1001&#xAE;,&nbsp;Lava&#xAE;</font><font style="display: inline;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">and Solvol&#xAE;. &nbsp;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0.1pt 0pt;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#xFEFF;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0.1pt 0pt;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">Headquartered in San Diego, WD-40 Company recorded net sales of $423.4 million in fiscal year 2019 and its products are currently available in more than 176 countries and territories worldwide. WD-40 Company is traded on the NASDAQ Global Select market under the ticker symbol &#x201C;WDFC.&#x201D; For additional information about WD-40 Company please visit</font><font style="display: inline;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;text-decoration:underline;">http://www.wd40company.com</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">.</font>
